  no ingested thread reaches a post-Gilded era (`tea1772` stalls at 1874 despite
  its "to future" title; `hd`/`drums`/`pop` top out in Gilded/Progressive/Populism).
  Is there a separate continuation thread carrying a campaign past ~1924? If not,
  the late/"future" eras remain undocumented and unbounded.
- **Dual era-scoring formula** (`tea1772`/#102): the per-era winner + cumulative
  "winner of the game so far" are *announced* at each boundary but the **point
  formula is not shown** in `tea1772` (closest is `rep1800` POST 6201). What banks
  vs resets across bands, and is the cumulative bank the canonical win condition?
- **Two sequential 1772 drafts?** (`new1772`/§2a): the forum runs an **Inaugural
  Draft (established pols) THEN a separate Rookie Draft** in 1772; shipped
  `scenario1772` does ONE snake draft. Does the build model two sequential drafts?
- **First-President unopposed rule** (`new1772`/#104): is the Celebrity+Military-
  Leader "unopposed on d6 4-6, resolved before the other party nominates" rule
  canonical, and does it generalize beyond the very first presidential election?
- **SCOTUS-overturns-an-Amendment** (`tea1772`/#100): is Gov-requested judicial
  review of a *ratified Amendment* (→ repeal/revert) a real shipped mechanic, and
  what reverses it (re-pass by Congress)?
- **SCOTUS ruling → statute cascade** (`tea1772`/DH-41): vcczar explicitly deferred
  the Prigg cascade — does a ruling that contradicts a law on the books void/neuter
  that law, or leave it operative (the current default)?
- **Stat-floor → forced presidential resignation** (`tea1772`/#105): the exact
  floor (all-Command + "most" skills) that forces a sitting Pres to resign.
- **Post-12A legislature-state vote count** (`new1772`/DH-44): Kingmaker votes vs
  Gov+Senators+focus-Reps headcount — which is canonical? (also a `rep1800`/`hd` Q)
- **Late-ratification / "Rogue Island" path** (`new1772`/DH-38): does the build
  model abstaining/late-ratifying states + a multi-year amendment window, or pull
  decliners in as the founding-era thread did?
- **★ Senate pass-threshold** (`nuke`/#112 + DH-54-adjacent): does the Senate use a
  **~60% supermajority TO PASS** (≈58–59 of 96–98), or **simple-majority-to-pass with
  60% being CLOTURE only** (67%/65 for amendments)? The `nuke` mid-digests genuinely
  CONFLICT — one reports a built-in 60% pass threshold, another says the GM mis-ran a
  60% pass threshold and corrected it to simple-majority-to-pass with ~60% as cloture
  — and the rules text ("procedural rules may establish stricter rules") is ambiguous.
  **Needs the codebase / human to settle pass-vs-cloture before any Senate-floor work.**
  (`nuke` POST 2746-2770, 8155, 8308)
- **SEAM to the successor thread `3a9ac985` (2004→2020)** (`nuke`): the `nuke` thread
  software-truncated at ~2005 mid-page-cap and the GM opened the `modern` (2004→2020)
  continuation. Read them as one 1948→2020 campaign; the open ends of `nuke` (does the
  USSR ever fall? does the Era of Terror formally end at 2012? what is the named band
  after it?) are the likely subject of a **future batch ingesting `3a9ac985` as the
  PREDECESSOR-completed continuation.**
- **★ Boot Command** (`dem1820`/#115): do inaugural-draft pols keep their dataset
  Command, or is Command zeroed below an age/office threshold at boot? The GA stripped
  Command from ≤40 boot pols w/o a job — a contested, undocumented house rule
  ("nobody should be born with command"). The scenario-boot pipeline must decide.
- **★ Scenario-boot PROCEDURE** (`dem1820`/#115): there are **no documented rules for
  CREATING a game** — what is the canonical deterministic setup algorithm (strip-Command
  decision, inaugural career-track seed from the last-3-classes, era-keyed industry
  init, Senate-class assignment + verifier, vacant-seat fill, 5+5 ideology ladder +
  era-tuned decks)? The build's boot pipeline IS the missing spec.
- **★ Player-controlled SCOTUS — built or not?** (`dem1820`/#52 vs `pop` POST 479-480):
  `dem1820` runs a LIVE player-controlled court (votes by-ideology-chart, but
  delay/dismiss is a player action; dismiss only Gov-Action cases; must hear ≥1) —
  which RE-ENABLES the control `pop` said vcczar disabled mid-design. Is the court
  all-CPU or player-controllable-with-restrictions? The design is unsettled.
- **★ Meter→election enthusiasm model FORK — PARTLY RESOLVED** (`dem1820`/#18/#51 →
  `arkzag`): the **`arkzag` continuation SETTLED the enthusiasm-SHIFT step** to the
  canonical `drums` 4-step rule (faction MOST-pts-for-dominant +1 / LEAST −1 / MOST-pts-
  for-opposition +1-toward-dominant / LEAST-pts-from-opposition +2-toward-opposition;
  shifts stack), **NOT** Ted's "every state" or Matt's "primaries only." The **remaining
  #18 open piece** is purely the meter→election *state-application* step (does a per-
  ideology-card bonus apply to every state unless penalized, or only ideology-leaning
  states?).
- **★ Convention delegate-class assignment: human-rigged or AI-auto?** (`arkzag`/#13):
  Zagnut moved delegate-class assignment to **AI-auto** (a published 5-category EV×1..×4
  formula) to kill self-dealing + save time, but Ted holds delegate-**rigging is intended
  design** — and the **1840 convention reverted to human-set classes**. The build must
  pick: an AI/deterministic delegate allocator, or a player-set one (with the rigging as
  a feature)?
- **★ Acting-president scope** (`arkzag`/#61): when a successor (e.g. Enoch Lincoln) is
  an **acting president** — or a trait (Easily Overwhelmed) diverts their actions to the
  VP — what exactly can/can't they do (exec actions, SCOTUS compels, signing bills)? The
  arkzag arc only shows the action-divert roll, not the full power set.
- **House focus-Rep incumbency** (`dem1820`/#55 vs vcczar POST 704): the per-thread
  ruling is seat-locked incumbency except census/redistricting years — but vcczar's
  long-term wish is full per-district simulation (+30k pols). Which does the build model?
- **Career-track run/appoint eligibility** (`dem1820`/#86/DH-25/DH-56): 2.1 says CT pols
  "can't run or be appointed," but many sections pull them by election/appointment; the
  GA ruled to ignore the bar. The build must pick ONE coherent rule (and the appointment
  order — own-party-not-CT → own-party-CT → opposite-not-CT → opposite-CT → generate?).
- **★ CPU draft ideology-distance** (`oopscpu`/OC-4/#72): should the CPU draft be gated on
  ideology distance (a 2.1.6-style pliable + same/adjacent gate) so a left faction can't
  headhunt Andrew Jackson (RW Pop), or should draft restrictions be relaxed wholesale? Ted
  wants "a better third way" than (a) off-ideology draftee can never lead vs (b) strong
  pol uncontested. **Build call.**
- **CPU crisis-vote-against-self** (`oopscpu`/OC-3/#74): how should a CPU vote on a crisis
  bill that costs its own cards? Current rule is too generous (peaceful 1792 abolition,
  no secession check). Tighten support-by-harm + add a pre-resolve secession/era check.
- **What counts as "an office"** for the office-holder / non-office-holder event target
  pools (`oopscpu`/OC-8/#140): career track? a bare faction/party leader? Needs a canonical
  predicate + an event-text fix.
- **Can a pol run for both Governor and President/VP in the pre-primary era?**
  (`oopscpu` POST 238-244): allowed here "since there's no campaigning"; the "Booker Rule"
  gov action that would govern this is discussed but may not exist. Pin a stated rule.

## Sources

Sources are now split into **playtest threads** (continuous narrative threads
of an actual game-in-progress — the primary source for mechanics in play) and
**discussion threads** (community-curated fix-catalogs / rule-clarification
threads — secondary, but the primary source for **dataset accuracy**, small
mechanical bugs, and designer rulings on rules ambiguity).

### Playtest threads (ingested digests)

### Discussion threads (community-curated catalogs; the dataset-accuracy source)

A *separate* class of source from the playtest threads. Discussion threads are
**not** game-in-progress narratives — they are running community-curated lists
of small fixes (dataset bugs, mechanical typos, designer-ruling clarifications)
that the build inherits as fix-it tickets, not as gameplay-validation. **Do not
confuse with playtest threads** — there are no GA rulings on a running game
here; there are designer rulings on policy/dataset Qs.

- [`cf82a7d3-a-thread-for-small-low-priority-changes-and-errors`](playtest-digests/cf82a7d3-a-thread-for-small-low-priority-changes-and-errors.md)
  (`smallbugs`) — **804 posts / 10 chunks** (single-pass reduce — a 3-year+
  community catalog of polish-tier fixes). Started Apr 2023 by @Imperator Taco
  Cat with the explicit charter "not… major changes to game rules or systems
  but fixing small errors"; ongoing through May 2026. The **primary source for
  dataset accuracy and small mechanical bugs.** Each entry is a one-line
  hand-off to the build, typically acknowledged within 1-2 reply posts by
  @MrPotatoTed, @vcczar, or @Arkansas Progressive and either "fixed inline" in
  the master sheet or deferred to "when Anthony codes that rule." **Headline
  contributions:** ~50 named-pol fixes, ~30 mechanical fixes, ~20 dataset
  additions (gap-log row **#120** umbrella) — all going via
  `scripts/seedDataset.mjs` `CURATED_ROWS` overrides; one NEW dataset gap
  (**#121 — Secessionist trait missing**); one NEW rules gap (**#122 — Pardon
  mechanics unspecified**); one late-modern content-fixes bundle (**#123**).
  **Designer-ruling distillate (§5 of digest):** Sept-2024 Ted batch of 8
  proposed rule changes (Pres-uses-Command-for-blunder hybrid adopted; Iron-Fist
  PL no-block / Disharmonious-or-Independent only-challenger gate adopted; etc.);
  **POST 734-735 is the channel through which the #38 relocation-cap-4 change
  was sent to Anthony for the build** (12-30-25, "Approved by vczar"). Strongly
  **corroborates DH-27 (trait-conflict slips in boot data, 3rd thread), DH-51
  (modern-pol overpowered recency bias, 3rd thread), DH-53 (bill→meter
  effect-table sign bugs, 4th thread), DH-60 (era-events fire without
  territory/asset prereqs, 2nd thread)**. Use as the **input catalog for one
  dataset-maintenance pass**.

- [`a0f0bf04-discussion-teds-change-log-of-doom`](playtest-digests/a0f0bf04-discussion-teds-change-log-of-doom.md)
  (`tedchange`) — **408 posts / 7 chunks** (single-pass reduce — a
  designer-led decision-log). **★ The AUTHORITATIVE channel for current rule
  wording in the entire forum corpus.** Started Sept 18 2024 by @MrPotatoTed
  as the FEEDBACK channel for his parallel "Change Log of Doom" thread, which
  enumerated the rule changes Ted was considering. The thread runs a
  **section-by-section systematic rules-doc cleanup pass from phase 2.1 →
  2.6** between Sept 2024 and Mar 2025, then **resumes Oct 2025** on a
  Lingering script clarification. Each section gets a Ted draft + 5-15
  pushback/refinement posts + a Ted final ruling + write to rules doc.
  **Critical context — Anthony coded ALONGSIDE this thread**, meaning rulings
  here are the LATEST shipped-design-intent the programmer was targeting.
  **Headline contributions:** ~25 NEW gap rows (#124-#142) and ~10 RESOLUTIONS
  of OPEN questions / SUPERSESSIONS of prior digest interpretations. **The
  canonical 2-step Pres implementation Admin-then-Command rule (POST 163)** is
  the authoritative wording of cf82a7d3 §5a #3. **★ Key NOT-touched items:**
  the relocation-cap-4 ruling, the amendments-not-SCOTUS-challengeable rule,
  the Civil-Rights-Act-not-repealable decision — those are 12a's (cf82a7d3)
  domain. The two discussion threads have **complementary scope**: 12a =
  playtest-bug catalog; 12b = section-by-section systematic rewrite.
  **SUPERSESSIONS** (Ted's rulings override prior GA reads): Kingmaker vs
  Master Kingmaker bonus scope (was "either-or" per Matt's reading; now
  Kingmaker = state-only / Master = every-state-incl-own, POST 316); 3+3
  random-traits + random-alt-states draft count (was 5/5 in earlier reads,
  now 3/3, POST 50); the Hale=1/2-death + ex-Pres-only-rolls-death rules
  close the John-Adams-immortality loop (POST 143, 396). **Open items at
  thread end:** Mil-Prep meter level 4 fix (independently re-discovered but
  NOT closed), Universal Election Modifier proposal, Crisis-trait
  consolidation, faithless-elector wording rework, term-limit Gov-action
  era-gating. **NO conflict with batch-9 review-gate Senate cloture ruling**
